Traffic:+-
This really depends on the time of day. When I go during store operating hours, customers can really be impatient and unfriendly: blocking others, trying to cut in line with different driving styles "and licenses." When getting gas during less crowded hours, things flow much smoother.

Appearance:+++

<review>I've lived in Boyle Heights & East L.A. forever & never knew this place existed, I came across it on IG one of my most favorite foods in gyros but they have to have the meat that is carved in restaurant not that gross frozed pre formed garbage that some "Mediterranean restaurants" sell..I ordered the Gyro which came served with a side salad, pickled beets & a pepperoncini and I also ordered the Gyro Mix which is gyro meat,chx kabob,beef kabob, hummus, & a side salad with 1 pita bread...also ordered an order of churros they were pictured as a bag with small churros but it only ended up being 1 regular sized churro & it had a bavarian type filling which was not stated on their google map page...both combos were for myself as I was sampling their meats as I was thinking of ordering catering for Friday...all the food was perfect even the presentation in their to-go boxes, all meats were seasoned & tender (beef is extremely tender you can pull pieces straight off the kabob), rice was fluffy, plates came with 2 sauces definately the green sauce is the best...highly recommended! Something about Mediterranean food that leaves you content & satisfied (not overstuffed) maybe it's the fresh ingredients<//review>< Date>

< review>
I am sooooooo excited The Pupper Club Petit is open for business! Took my doggo in yesterday for a little bath time action and they FAR exceeded my expectations!!! My doggo got a facial, complete with drops in the eyes to avoid any burning/eye watering and then a good ole scrub a dub dub! Once he was all sudsy and rinsed, he got a nice blow dry and several applications of wonderfully smelling sprays to brighten his coat and freshen his scent... I had no idea doggo cologne existed! After all of this came a nice solid de-furmination!

My pup was so happy afterwards and got sooooo many compliments on his scent (he actually made my apartment smell more fresh!!) I also asked if they would file his nails, but Sam, the groomer, let me know that he didn't need it... no pressured up selling here! Just sincere people who really love dogs! I know where we'll be getting our baths from now on!

I had went a placed an order online to buy my husband a Simpson helmet as Christmas gift. I had called the phone number provided in the website to ask about the return policy since it was a Christmas gift and my husband most likely was going to get it on Christmas Day. Little did I know the size I order was XL and found out my husband current helmet size was L. Called Eddie to see if I could change the size to a L before it shipped. He was super nice and made it happen. Once the helmet arrived hubby received it so no more waiting until Christmas Day! (Since he works from home). Found out that the size L in that specific type of helmet was a little big still. Also the hubby is a little picky and hard to find the right present he decided he wanted a M Matte black instead of the glossy he got! Called Eddie and he went above and beyond to get the size and the color as requested. Made it super easy for us to return the current helmet and get the new one super fast. Hands down amazing business and amazing customer service. <Rating>5</Rating>< text>
Dr. Dabaco is the best! I could tell you a million stories of how she's gone above and beyond while helping me and my cats, but instead I'll just tell you the story of the first time I met her - the day I decided I wanted her for my vet.

I was volunteering at a "Fix Our Ferals" clinic where Dr Dabaco was also volunteering her time and skills. Things were going smoothly when suddenly someone yelled "CRASH!", meaning a cat needed immediate help. I look up and see a very pregnant woman nimbly climb on top of an operating table and, with a look of singular determination, begin CPR on the cat. She worked very hard to save the kitty, but unfortunately whatever reaction he had had to the anesthesia was fatal. Still, what stuck in my memory was that if this woman would try THAT hard to save a plain old shorthaired black cat that didn't even have an owner...just imagine how hard she would work to help MY beloved babies (most of whom ARE "plain old shorthaired black cats").<//text>

I told him to go ahead and submit the supplemental claims to State Farm, so we could get going on the work. I waited a week and still heard nothing back from him. I called and Estafany, the receptionist, told me she would have him call me back. He never did.  I then wait another day or two and called back again. This time I got to speak to Isaac. He told me that he had done nothing with my estimated to State Farm and that he had "dropped the ball". He stated that it was because he didn't know how to submit the claims because there were two of them. I told him he should have called me to ask to call them, or call them himself. He never said he was sorry for the delay, just that he understood because I was unhappy with his service. <userid>108621951725667427915<//userid>< text>
Im typing this review the way that my experiance at this shop unfolded.

I went to this body shop based off of reviews on here and other sites. Issac, Lucy, and Katie come across as wonderful people and they were/are pleasant to deal with.

However, i cannot refer anyone to this shop based off of my experience here. I personally would not come back to get any of our vehicles repaired here unless its warranty work for the one that was fixed here.

When i initially picked up my vehicle (insurance job) after it was repaired, paint job was poor (specific areas were not painted, or painted properly), there was overspray on parts that normally do not have paint on them (trim pieces), parts were not reinstalled that were originally removed to repair the damage, vehicle was dirty, bondo-work could be seen through clear coat (you could tell which direction the bondo filler was sanded due to someone being to lazy to use a fine grit sandpaper to complete the job), license plate tag was removed/scrapped-off (this is ridiculous on so many levels), parts that should of been replaced were not replaced..in my opinion the vehicle was not completed in a timely manner and seemed to have been rushed at the end to be completed. I returned the vehicle to have the items above and more, repaired/addressed.

I understand some of the parts acquisition was out of the control of the shop, but i have the impression that the parts-searching could of been accomplished a little more "stream-lined" (utilize more sources such as other dealerships, research vehicle forums, research various online sites that sell parts, do better research locally within wrecking yards). I the customer shouldnt have to do research on my own (out of my own frustration)  and point you in the direction of where to acquire any part (i only did this to get my car finished).

When i picked up the vehicle the second time, all the items were addressed that i requested to be addressed, the vehicle was cleaned properly this time...there are some issues im not happy with regarding quality and finish on the paint in certain areas...but i can live with it.

Overall, Issac, Lucy, and Katie were pleasant to deal with. However, communication was poor based off of being told a few times that i would get a call back and it not happening, or not happening in a timely manner. Or being told that i would get a call back by one individual and actually getting a call back at another time by another individual. This i find to be un-professional.

I feel in the end that this shop can turn out awesome work....i've seen some of the vehicles in the shop and know that they can do better then what occured with my vehicle. It frustrates me why my car received sub-par treatment/work done to it and came  across as a rush job at the end (paint/body work wise).... maybe its the painter that was replaced shortyly after my vehicle was painted, who did a horrible job in my opinion, or maybe its to much work and not enough manpower or quality manpower, or maybe the lack of quality control led to my situation. Either way, i would never let a car leave my shop (if i were the owner) in the condition that i received mine initially and with the crappy work that was accomplished on it. I regret going here and not taking it elsewhere...i hate saying this because i was excited when i first dropped it off, and the owners are nice people. But this in the end turned out to be a nightmare.  Sorry about the long post, but this is a honest un-biased review which may shed light on someone else that who will be in my position of shopping around for a dependable shop to fix their vehicle.< /text>

<time>1529105209345<//time><rate>5<//rate><Resp>{'time': 1529771294790, 'text': 'We appreciate your review. We are continually striving to improve the customer experience. Thank you for your feed back!'}</Resp><user>109744494874869184826< /user>< review>
I have been going here since I was a child, however, even as an adult, I do nearly all of my shopping at this particular location, as it is both very high quality as well as convenient to my home.

The quality of the fruits, vegetables, and meats is unbeatable in the area, which are my must-haves for a grocery store, so this is the perfect store for me.

I often do my shopping around the same times, and the staff is super friendly, and most of them have gotten familiar enough to know me either by name or at least by face. Even the new staff is very friendly as well!

Be sure to become a member of their "Something Extra" rewards program. They will send you extra coupons via email, and also coupons as well as a cash voucher for a percentage of the amount of money you spend their each quarter. For me this is a big deal, as they are often personalized for the items that I actually buy there, rather than random coupons that might come in the mail.

Their prices for everyday items can at times be a littler higher. I actually don't mind this too much, as the quality of their perishable items is so high, the store is always clean, and I never have trouble finding things, that I have no need to shop anywhere else!</review>

<Text>I just have to write this review to express how amazing Raley's in the Natomas location is. Especially the Peet's Coffee crew and of course the Bakery department. I work at Great Clips in the shopping center and frequently visit Raley's. Thank you to Matt, Terry, Michelle, Angelica, Mary and whoever else I forgot to mention. Because they are all amazing.

This reveiw is so important to me for the upper management to see. Because my Son and I lives have been changed because of their kindness.

My Son is 20 years old and has a disability called 48xxyy Syndrome. We come to Raley's and Peet's Coffee on my days off for our weekly routine "lunch date" Leo looks forward to this every week, to visit "the guys". We grab coffee and lunch and eat in the deli area. It's always a good time. We small talk with them and leave full and happy. This being a huge accomplishment being that Leo isn't always the easiest guy to get along with.

April 1st was Leo's Birthday. I told the guys we would be coming in as usual. Not expecting anything but to hang out a little on Leo's Birthday. Well Matt went above and beyond. We arrived and Michelle told me that Matt had Angelica make Leo a cake. Such an awesome idea. So thoughtful and brought tears to my eyes. When he got back from lunch we all surprised Leo and sang him Happy Birthday. Leo felt so special. What a great feeling for a Mom!!

It makes me still beleive in people and kindness. To think of my Son on his birthday like that is so thoughtful. To make my special Son, Leo feel so happy. He loves you guys. Best beleive we will continue our "lunch dates".  The best part is Leo wouldn't eat his cake at home. He said "it's made with too much love, Mom" and that's how I know he was thankful.</Text>< Pictures>
